import jsonlines
import base64
import os
for f in os.listdir('./fisma_pdf_jsons'):
    reader = jsonlines.open(os.path.join('./fisma_pdf_jsons', f))
    lines = []
    for l in reader:
        lines.append(l)
    x = lines[-1]
    decoded_content = base64.b64decode(x['content']).decode('utf-8')
    print(decoded_content)
    with open(os.path.join('/Users/alina/Desktop', f.replace('jsonl', 'txt')), 'w+') as wf:
            for line in decoded_content:
                    wf.write(line)
